Free Talk

Madman (2) 250

— Ling He

Er Lai Zi, after breakfast, still brimming with excitement, headed to the east village. Along the way, he could hear snippets about the reason Wang Lao Si had gone mad, as many were discussing this news. However, this seemed unnecessary to him. "Seeing is believing," he thought, "why not go straight to Wang Lao Si's house to find out the truth?" With his mind made up, Er Lai Zi hurried towards the dog-mother's place.

In Er Lai Zi's eyes, the village indeed felt different today. Wang Lao Si's doorway, for example, was packed with people; he couldn't recall seeing such a crowd except during Wang Lao Si's wedding years ago.

Er Lai Zi was too short. Even on tiptoe, he only reached an adult's shoulder. He struggled, pushing through people's armpits. He saw Wang Lao Si sitting there, picking lice. This disappointed Er Lai Zi; the so-called madman was no different from ordinary people. He still had that same beard, dirty and ugly, and Er Lai Zi suspected it was filled with lice eggs. He wasn't doing anything out of the ordinary, just picking lice and popping them into his mouth. What was most disappointing was that he wasn't talking. What was the point of a madman who didn't talk? Really, there was nothing to see.

Many slowly dispersed, seemingly not particularly thrilled. Only the children remained. Er Lai Zi naturally didn't want to leave immediately; perhaps there would be something interesting later.

Sure enough, the madman stood up. The children suddenly jumped and ran off. Er Lai Zi also ran, but then thought, "Ha, now the show begins."

The madman ran out of the door, running forward and shouting loudly:

"Come on, everyone follow me, let's burn the motherfucker's house down!"

Burn a house? Whose house? No one knew. But these were the words of a madman; who would believe him? So no one took it seriously. But Wang Lao Si kept running, and many children followed him, some women who weren't very old, the large group, with great momentum, it was quite a lively scene. Burn a house? Really burn it? That would be interesting. So everyone followed along to watch the excitement, even Dog-Mother, who rarely left her house.

But unexpectedly, the madman Wang Lao Si stopped next to the ancestral hall. Of course, this was a new trick.

In the darkness of the ancestral hall's corridor, a pitifully thin old female dog was giving birth in a pile of dry grass. Two pups had already been born, their bodies covered in a greasy membrane. Another pup's head was already out, and the mother only needed one more push to bring it completely into the world. However, the dog was holding on to her last breath, and she didn't have the strength.

The madman was now staring at them, his eyes gleaming with a terrible ferocity, but the children were very happy. They saw the little lives moving slightly, clapping their hands and laughing innocently. Only the women knew the dog-mother's pain and felt great pity for the skinny dog.

"Oh! Maybe the little dog will never be born!..."

(To be continued)

Unspoken Understanding 251

— Yang Chun

Ever since the fall of Yuguan and the tension at Shimen, we've been able to read in the newspapers generals' passionate telegrams expressing their readiness to fight. From those in power to those out of office, from army commanders to brigade commanders, telegrams fly back and forth in a flurry of activity, everyone eager to "not lag behind others in saving the country." Even the "Liu Family Generals," busy with street fighting and close combat, sent a telegram expressing their "cessation of internal warfare, ready to fight." Even General Liu Zhennian, known for his achievements in Yantai, telegraphed Beijing a few days ago, volunteering to lead his troops north to resist the Japanese. The central government, as always, responded to these passionate requests with "warm encouragement," or replies like "await further instructions." Especially for General Liu Zhennian, in addition to "warm encouragement," they also urged him to "strive for reconstruction." These responses echoed each other in perfect harmony, like listening to a deep bell.

Originally, to "resist" was said to be "long-term." The central government's true intentions, as clever as generals are, how could they not know? Knowing full well that their "volunteering" would not be "approved," they insisted on "volunteering" anyway. This way, they could create a false impression and show that they "do not lag behind others in saving the country," how wonderful! And as insightful as the central government is, they also knew the generals' intentions, and knew even better that even if their "volunteering" were "approved," the generals would never resolutely lead their troops north, so it was better to do a favor and send a warm, encouraging reply with a "!?!" This way, they could show that the central government had already planned, and also make the generals admire the central government's wisdom. Everything was unspoken, and the mutual understanding resonated with harmonious sounds throughout the nation!

However, besides a pair of ears, the people also have a pair of eyes that can see clearly! "What everyone sees, what everyone points at," the harmonious ensemble, the farcical duet, ultimately cannot anesthetize the people's souls!

Sickness 252

— Ms. Bing

I'm sick, I'm really sick now.

When a person is sick, their temper and mood are completely different from when they are well. Nothing can spark their interest, they have no hope, they can't even feel emotions for their closest relatives. There is only boredom, only depression, only thoughts of death, and the feeling that everything in the world is empty.

Ah, sickness, it's truly terrifying!

Rich people are not afraid of sickness. No matter what illness they have, they can be cured. They have money to stay in the hospital, money for surgery, money for medicine, money for injections, money for tonics. If they don't like the sanatoriums in Moganshan or West Lake in China, they can go to foreign countries in a flash, how carefree! But what about those who have no money? Not only can they not afford to see a doctor or rest, but they still have to work desperately. If they don't, what will they live on? No one wants to starve to death lying down!

Alas! What's the use of saying these useless words? I'm sick, but what can I do? Sick is still sick, isn't it?

It's too painful, really. I feel that nothing in the world is more painful than sickness! Beheading, shooting, these are momentary pains, but sickness, no matter how long it lasts, is always more painful than beheading or shooting. A healthy person lying in bed, unable to move, can only endure the pain. Thinking about the people outside laughing happily, walking vigorously, working hard at their jobs, beautiful hopes smiling and beckoning to them. But what about me? I can't do anything, I have nothing, I can only wait for the god of death to come and take me quietly to hell, as if I had taken sleeping pills.

However, that would be too cheap for my enemies if I really died of sickness.

On "Suicide" 253

— Ms. Cao Ruhui

In recent days, newspapers have been filled with news about suicide. Some are due to grief and anger about national affairs, some are due to economic hardship, and some are due to romantic desires. Some say that suicide is an act of courage, a beautiful destruction. Schopenhauer also said, "What's wrong with suicide?" I am absolutely against this view. I believe that suicide is an absolutely cowardly act, because those who commit suicide simply do not have the courage to face darkness and "cruelty," and especially do not have the determination to fight against "darkness" and "cruelty."

I think there should be two explanations for "life": one is "existence" and the other is "living." The former is without will and purpose, "existing in the world," while the latter is "living" with "vitality" and purpose. In this world, there are originally many people like walking corpses, like shadows, like ghosts, who only occupy a position in space and have absolutely no "vitality of life." They live only for enjoyment, for plundering the fruits of other people's labor. Such life is naturally worse than death. My view on such life is:

"A life like clinging leaves is not as good as a death like fallen flowers!"

What's more, their lives are not even as good as withered leaves, because withered leaves at least don't plunder the moisture and fertilizer of new leaves. If such lives were accelerated to death, I would naturally be twelve points in favor.

But most of those who commit suicide today are not well-fed walking corpses, nor are they devils who plunder the fruits of the labor of the masses, but are oppressed people, prisoners in the dungeons of darkness and cruelty. The oppressed and the prisoners have vitality, they are the supporters of the world, so they should not commit suicide, they should only fight! For themselves, for the people, for the future of history.

Why are national affairs in such a state? Why is life so pressing? Extending to unrequited love, heartbreak, etc., one should always ask "why"? This world is originally too dark, there are too many unexpected events, and there are only cries of pain, groans, hunger and cold, the wails of the weak and the songs of the strong echoing in space. But you must ask why is it like this? Why is this world dark? You should find a perpetrator? You should find an enemy? After being whipped by the devil, jumping into the Huangpu River, or drinking a cup of sleeping pills, is what kind of cowardice? I believe that only the brave can face darkness and cruelty, and only the brave can seek light from darkness and find happiness from cruelty. Suicide, why? For others? For yourself? The strong are sending out mocking and victorious laughs at your cowardly blood, and your death is enough to prolong the time of darkness. Madame Roland once said: "I will not commit suicide; if I commit suicide, I will kill a few villains first!" Here, I further affirm: "I will not commit suicide! I will resolutely fight against the darkness to the last moment of life!"

Only a death in struggle is a courageous death, a beautiful death, a meaningful and valuable death! Suicide, why? For yourself? For the people?

Therefore, I firmly oppose suicide! Because it is a bucket of cold water poured on the flames of struggle!

Artificial Snowflakes 254

—

Nature can no longer proudly say: "I can create beautiful and mysterious snowflakes." Now, in fact, we can create snowflakes that are the same as those created by nature.

The first person to study this amazing phenomenon was John Mead Adams, a physics professor at the University of California. He made snowflakes by hand and observed their changes.

The manufacturing method is: first mix two kinds of air, one kind of air is dry and the temperature is below freezing, and the other kind of air is humid and the temperature is higher. When these two kinds of air are mixed, snowflakes are created and fall one by one. Finally, they fall into a small hole where they can be observed, and then a microscope is used to take pictures and observe the snowflake's organizational order.

When snowflakes are first formed, they are like a kind of crystal, and their diameter is only four ten-thousandths of an inch. Even if fifteen snowflake particles are arranged together, they are not as wide as a hair on a person's body. The simplest shape is a hexagonal prism, with the height and width almost equal. When the snowflakes increase in size, their shape remains unchanged until they reach more than ten times their original shape, and then they begin to change shape. Sometimes, when increasing in size, two snowflakes combine together to form a long prism, but its interior is empty, like a tooth that has been damaged by worms, or it forms a form that has ended.

Remarks

Snow 256

— Wu

Again it snows, a white shroud covering the entire earth, filling the poor with boundless dread. However, because "snow heralds a bountiful year," old scholars, cradling their pipes and stroking their beards, gaze upon the white landscape, filled with great hope; ["Perhaps next year will be another harvest? But Mencius said, 'A life of ease often ends in hardship,' alas!"] they sigh deeply.

Because the snow reflects silver light, the vast world, a dazzling sight, talents who create art for art's sake cannot help but be inspired. ["Ah! This sacred earth, I wish to be buried beneath it forever, eternally, forever dwelling in this ivory tower."]

Because the snow scene is enchanting, our sentimental young masters, of course, hold their beloved, speeding in cars across the snowy ground, their hearts ablaze with fiery passion; ["My love! Look, Heaven has adorned us with such beauty, how can we not enjoy it in time?"] A wild kiss, how sweet those crimson lips.

Because snowflakes, after all, bring a clear fragrance, and life offers few chances for appreciation, our esteemed committee members, amidst their protests and telegrams, cannot help but have their refined spirits stirred. They go to the park, to the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum, taking photos and filming scenes, and composing verses, undoubtedly masterpieces, both elegant and achieving fame.

Although the methods of enjoying oneself may differ, the leisurely mood is the same.

However, as the heavy snow falls, what of the patriotic heroes?

The Northeast Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army, clad in thin clothing and barefoot in the freezing snow, carrying saddles to keep warm, valiantly resist the enemy. Ultimately, lacking both support and supplies, they inevitably suffer defeat, death, or flight. Seeing the enemy deeply penetrating Yu (Liaoning), plundering North China, how can one not be heartbroken?

So, are the people in the rear truly without money to provide aid? How much is gambled away at a roulette table? How much does a fox fur coat cost? How much is spent on a Taoist ritual? How much is spent on grand weddings and funerals? So, is the government truly powerless to provide support? How much do guns, cannons, and bullets cost with each internal conflict? How many planes roar through the skies of the interior? How many soldiers "lie dead across the fields" and "blood flows like rivers," sacrificed in civil wars? How much is each compensation or state funeral fee issued to warlords? Therefore, it is not that they cannot, but that they will not.

Therefore, at this time when the world is a blinding white and we... (incomplete sentence), we should not harbor any illusions. If we truly love China, we should shoulder our guns and rush to the front lines, organized and disciplined, to fight for the future of our nation!

Science

Dyeing Cotton, Wool, and Silk Fabrics with Basic Dyes 257

— Zhan Neng

The dyeing of various fabrics such as cotton, wool, and silk has become an extremely important issue today, perhaps because of its extensive applications!

The earliest inventors of dyeing techniques were our Chinese ancestors! This can be verified by ancient history. Back then, emperors, kings, dukes, lords, and the common people of our country had different colors for their clothing. The prevalence of dyeing techniques at that time can be imagined. Unfortunately, each dynasty regarded industry as a lowly profession, adhering to old methods without seeking improvement, leading to the decline we see today!

In 1859, artificial dyes gradually developed, and dyeing techniques were influenced by this, becoming a branch of the chemical industry. From then on, chemical theories and scientific methods were used to research and improve dyeing, leading to the latest dyeing industry of today.

The above is some introduction to this article. Now we can get to the main text.

Several commonly used dyes in basic dye dyeing are as follows.

Red: Fuchsin Cerise Safranin

Yellow: Phosphine Auramine Chrysidine

Green: Malachite Green J

Blue: Aniline Blue Methylene Blue Induline

Purple: Methyl Violet Crystal Violet

Brown: Marron Bismarck Brown

The colors dyed with this type of basic dye are extremely vibrant. This dye can also be used to dye different materials together, resulting in unusually bright and harmonious colors. Unfortunately, it is not very resistant to light. Only two blue dyes, Laduline Methylene Blue, have strong light resistance.

When dyeing, it is not advisable to add the dye solution all at once; it should be added in two or three successive increments. Basic dyes should not be mixed with acidic dyes, as insoluble precipitates may occur, which will stain the fabric, and the resulting color will not be even. This should be noted.

Basic Dyeing Method for Cotton.

First, the cotton fabric should undergo mordanting treatment with acidic substances such as gallnut and catechu to make the color durable.

For the mordanting method, the cotton fabric can be soaked in hot water, wrung dry, and immersed in a solution of mordant. Let it sit for twelve to twenty-four hours, squeeze dry, and immerse it in a solution of antimony salt, such as tartar emetic. (This substance is easily soluble in water and requires the addition of a small amount of sodium carbonate to neutralize the free acid in order to preserve it.) Then, antimony tannate is formed, which is fixed to the fiber.

After being mordanted, the cotton fabric is immersed in a weakly basic dye solution and heated to 60 degrees Celsius. The fixed tannic acid reacts with the dye to form tannin antimony oxychloride, which has very strong adhesion, hence its excellent washing and soap resistance.

After dyeing, rinse with clean water. That's it. (The amount of dye and mordant is fixed and based on the weight of the fabric.)

Basic Dyeing Method for Wool.

This dyeing method does not require auxiliary agents and can directly dye the fabric, making it easy to obtain even colors.

During dyeing, the dye solution can be heated to around 30 degrees Celsius, and then the woolen fabric is immersed. Gradually increase the temperature to 80 degrees Celsius and keep it there for one hour before removing and cleaning it. This method should not use boiling hot dye.

Because wool absorbs color faster at high temperatures than at low temperatures, the resulting color gloss is inferior.

Adding a small amount of Marseilles soap to the dye solution can result in extremely vibrant colors. However, the dyeing temperature should not exceed 50 degrees Celsius. First, mix the soap with water and boil thoroughly, then filter out the resulting viscous foam before applying it, otherwise, the finished product will have mottled spots and stains, which is very unsightly.

Basic Dyeing Method for Silk.

Silk can also absorb basic dyes at room temperature, so its dyeing method is the same as that for wool fabrics. However, it is advisable to add raw silk soap (a soap solution containing dissolved sericin) to the dye solution to make the color more even. The dye solution temperature should not exceed 50 degrees Celsius.

Sacrifice 258

— Shen Zhou

["Kill! Kill! Kill!"]

["Clatter, clatter, clatter..."] Enemy iron birds

["Disperse the whole team!"]

["Hiss! Hiss!... Boom!... Splash!......"]

["Ah!"]

["What? Gang, are you injured? Where? ... Where?"] Yong sees his comrade Gang fall to the ground and roll around. He hurriedly puts down his gun and goes forward to help him.

["Alas! Yong!... Left arm."]

Yong lifts Gang's arm and rests it on his own thigh. Gang's arm has been blown into a hole, the bone seems to be broken! The flesh is a blur, and blood keeps gushing out. He hurriedly unties his leggings and bandages Gang's arm. Gang keeps groaning in pain.

["Yong!... Water,... my mouth is dry!"]

["The water's here! Open your mouth!"] Yong unties the military hot water bottle from his waist and pours it into Gang's mouth. Gang uses his right hand to take the hot water bottle.

["Do you feel better?"]

["Uh, alas! Yong! I didn't expect to be injured! Alas! Damned enemy, I must kill you all! Or, maybe I can't kill you all, but there are my many comrades and countrymen. There are 400 million countrymen, they will provide us with bullets and rations, but our weapons need to be improved. Just now the gun I was using hasn't been fired for long, but the firing pin got so hot that it was impossible to fire. Although we have enthusiasm and perseverance, we suffered a lot from the enemy because of this... Alas!

Alas!"] Gang groans in pain.

["Da, da, da... Clap! Clap!... Rumble! Rumble!"]

["Alas! Our government is always calm! Most countrymen are patriots in word only, saving the country on paper. I, Wang (?), can't say what kind of patriot I am, but at least in such a critical situation, I think that to save the country, one must come to the front line and fight the enemy to the death! Even more ridiculous are those so-called angry-at-the-country suicides. They are angry at the country and commit suicide, so the enemy returned the three northeastern provinces and retreated to the three islands? Why not bury their bodies on the battlefield? Perhaps, if they didn't die in battle, the enemy would be driven back by them? Ah! Alas!......"]

["Gang! You need to go to the rear to recuperate!"]

["No, I still want to fight! My right hand is not injured, and besides, I came here to sacrifice myself. It doesn't matter if I sacrifice myself, only after sacrifice can there be success. Yong, when you came here, weren't you holding a spirit of determination to die? This, I think, is the glory of the great Chinese nation, I hope that all countrymen have this determination!... Determination!...... Ah! Yong!... I... sacrificed myself,... I wish you..."] Gang tosses and turns, struggles until he is still.

["Gang! Hey! Gang! Ah, damned enemy, alas!"] Yong puts down Gang, picks up his gun, and goes forward.

Alley Pilgrimage 259

— Fu

| My House Experience |

One evening, we decided to move. Because this small front building could no longer accommodate all of us—my old brother, Lao Wang, and Mr. and Mrs. Zhang. Naturally, the first to propose it was my old brother, because my old brother was the leader of our group. He spent all his time writing manuscripts, and recently, because of the addition of more people, he really couldn't sit comfortably. Moreover, the landlady downstairs often gambled on roulette and mahjong and lost her temper, crying loudly in the middle of the night. We all felt very inconvenient. After my old brother proposed it that night, Lao Wang and I immediately seconded him. We immediately decided to set off early the next morning to look for a house. We assumed the French Concession in the west as our area, a pavilion room on the first floor as our target house, and twenty-five yuan per month as our standard rent.

The next morning, after everyone finished chewing on fried dough sticks, we only left Mrs. Zhang to watch the house. The four of us jumped on the tram and marched mightily to the French Concession. We were all from out of town, and everything was "inexplicable." My old brother was more experienced, so he led the way. Walking to the corner of Avenue Joffre and Rue Cardinal Luling, my old brother picked up his glasses and saw a rental advertisement on a telephone pole in the right corner. He called Lao Wang to go over and take a look, but it turned out to be a red paper strip for "serious cold for sale." Although there was a "rent" sign next to the red paper strip, it did not meet the "target house" principle. Looking at another one, he rushed in regardless of everything. A very beautiful Russian young woman came out and greeted us in fluent English. My old brother also spoke to her in broken English, but the Russian woman ignored my old brother and kept looking at Lao Wang, who was wearing a western suit. Lao Wang, who was usually eloquent, was so anxious that he was like an ant on a hot pot. He simply couldn't speak a word of English. Later, we learned that the rent was more than forty-five taels, so we turned around and ran away. From then on, we didn't know how many roads we walked, how many alleys we went through, how many times we knocked on doors, how many flights of stairs we climbed, how many kinds of languages we heard, how many kinds of strange shapes we saw, and how many kinds of smells we smelled. In this way, we didn't return home until late at night, still "unintelligible," only to get a cold laugh from Mrs. Zhang.

The next day, the third day, we continued to work hard, but we learned a lesson from experience. We realized that it was more convenient to have the pretty-boy Lao Wang lead the way, so my old brother had to take a backseat. We kept looking, but we kept finding nothing. Although we felt the sadness of disillusionment, we also had comfort; because in order to find a house, we had inspected the general family situation of Shanghai society. Mr. Zhang even brought a small notebook and recorded the experience in it at any time. Curious interest encouraged us, and we simply forgot our purpose. We were no longer anxious, without worries. In the past three days, we probably found thirty-two houses. These thirty-two houses generally met our ideals, but no one met the standard rent. According to Mr. Zhang's statistics;

More than forty-five yuan three More than forty-five taels one

More than forty yuan five

More than thirty-five yuan eight

More than thirty yuan fifteen

Total thirty-two

The most common number was thirty-four or five yuan, but this number was really too far from our standard, we could only sigh! Even when we were sighing, we were scolded by the young ladies. Even so, the secret rooms and caves of [Shanghai families] gave us a pleasant tour, Yanhua Cave, Zhulin Fang, and brothels, it seemed that we had all seen them. People from all over the country were there, but Southerners, especially people from Suzhou, were the most numerous (this naturally only applies to those who contacted us directly). According to statistics;

Suzhou people thirteen

Ningbo people eight

Shanghai people seven

Jiangbei people two

Beijing people one

Russian people one

Total thirty-two

Among them, somehow, women were the most numerous, this was a fact. But this was also a truly incredible fact. Mr. Zhang's statistics book says;

Young girls or women thirteen

Middle-aged women five

Old women three

Middle-aged men three

Young men one

Children or maids two

Men and women interviewed together five

Total thirty-two

This was really something we didn't expect. In three days, we would see so many different kinds of women? Barefoot, wearing slippers, disheveled, heavily made-up, smoke-filled. Please see the statistical table; (we met 26 women, see the table above)

Smoke-filled two

Heavily made-up five

Barefoot wearing slippers ten

Disheveled two

Rich People's Winter Life 260

—

Shop Clerk Correspondence

Two Questions About Natural Science 261

Editor:

Since your newspaper added the Shop Clerk Correspondence, our generally ignorant shop clerks can get considerable answers to difficult questions. This is really the gospel of society! I now have two questions about natural science to ask you.

Gold is obtained from sand or granite by panning or amalgamation. It does not contain toxic substances. Why does swallowing it cause death? And why can taking sheep neck bone charcoal allow it to pass safely out of the anus? What is the reason for the death, and what is the action of taking sheep neck bone charcoal?

Snow is formed by the condensation of water vapor when it encounters cold weather. This is true for winter snow, and it is no different for spring snow. But why do we welcome winter snow and hate spring snow? (The following is omitted)

Zhu Cinian

Editor's Note: After a person swallows gold, because the nature of gold is very heavy, it often stagnates in the intestines, leading to intestinal rupture and death. The small amount of gold leaf in our country's pills and powders will not kill people; and swallowing a large amount of metals other than gold will also lead to death; Ming is proof. It is not caused by toxic emissions, so the solution is simply to excrete it safely from the anus with the stool. There is no need for detoxification. It is found that bone charcoal (not limited to sheep neck bone) originally absorbs water in the intestines, making it extremely dry and increasing the ability to peristalsis to promote excretion. However, the power is too small and cannot have a ten-thousand-in-one grip. Zhu Jun, where did you get this method? We believe that when encountering a person who swallows gold, sending them to the hospital for treatment is the safest way!

Snow is a crystal formed by the condensation of water vapor encountering sudden cold. It is true that winter snow is the same as spring snow, but in winter, all the winter crops in the fields, their vitality is hidden in the underground roots, and the resistance is very strong; at the same time, the vitality of insects that harm crops and the eggs they leave behind is very weak. Therefore, winter snow does no harm to crops and can kill pests, but it is different in spring. The potential of plants develops outward, the branches and leaves sprout, and the resistance decreases accordingly; at the same time, the life of pests has turned, so spring snow not only cannot kill pests, but is enough to destroy crops. This is why we welcome winter snow and hate spring snow.

Movie Special

The Production Process of Grand Hotel 263

— He

(Below) The Book Account of Lionel Barrymore

This film also shows that Grast able to tell jokes. One day when Menno Val came to the photography farm of "Grand Hotel" to visit her, she had not yet arrived. This day, the "Grand Hotel" was filming the room of her room, so the electric door was put into a tree in a dress that released this hope. Later, Jia arrived and began rehearsals. She performed in an angry manner, while others were ambushing nearby waiting for Nova Luo to perform his drama.

The door of the clothing tree suddenly opened, and Jia was taken aback.

"Okay, are there any more people running out?" Jia asked, undoubtedly thinking of the old car of KeystodeKopo.

Just as we expected, there are many humorous places in this film. Jia sang a German song in this film, called IchLiebeDich, she used to sing this song Wu recalled for tuning to restore her memory. So I equipped her with a zither and a pianist.

Joan Crawford plays the role of a secretary, and in several scenes, she has to perform typing. Joan at home dedicated to a typewriter. Because she wanted to perform realistically, and only a certain typewriter could make her work like this. So the company found a new one for her and rented it to her.

At that time, John Barryham was very fond of several books brought out by the supply department. This was probably because these old-edition ancient books were the green reason he was collecting. He got the book he wanted. The price was paid unknowingly by his brother Lionel, because when the supply department asked him whether the book price should be put on the account. He was angry and said,

"No, I don't have any dealings with the company, my brother has a good account."

"Why do I have this book account?" Lionel roared in surprise a few days later "I have never bought a book."

"Aha, yes, you bought it," said his brother John "Bought it for me."

Lionel had to spend an hour every day transforming into the role of Kinking, the short and sickly German who was determined to get rid of his last moment in the "Grand Hotel".

Because, as already mentioned above, in this film, the "Grand Hotel" itself occupies the most prominent position and surpasses all the actors. All the actions are performed in the hotel. Everyone's life is subdued by the influence of the Grand Hotel, so when a waiter in a wine bar mixes a drink, when a maid tidies up a room, they are equally important.

In order to make this hotel detailed and without delay, there are no trivial matters left or flaws revealed. The instructions on each reception room are in German. The telephone office has the Berlin telephone office, that is, the flowers and plants in the flower shop are also arranged according to the latest pointed style in Berlin.

The Contribution of Film to Science 264

— Hua

Film certainly holds a very important position in science. The “Trip to the Moon,” produced by the Bird Company after two years of painstaking effort, is one example. According to the measurements of Professor Oberth of the University of Berlin, the distance between the Earth and the Moon is 1,343,520,000 meters. Thus, inventors have based their new theories on inventing rockets that can fly 11,200 meters per second, allowing humans to explore the Moon. "Trip to the Moon" depicts this great feat, and many of the fantastic images of space are not seen in other films. It is said that it will soon be released in Paris. I believe it can give them some new scientific knowledge.

Film Reviews

Review of "Northeast Volunteer Army: A Bloody War History" 265

— Ling He

Produced by Jinan Film Company

Premiered at the Beijing Grand Theatre

This is another film about the actual battles of the Northeast Volunteer Army.

Undoubtedly, in China today, films that encourage the people to fight for the nation are not at all too many. What harm would there be in having a few more?

Furthermore, "Northeast Volunteer Army: A Bloody War History," which was recently screened at the Central Theatre, was produced by Nine Star Company and is essentially the same type of work as this film. However, the advertisement at the Beijing Grand Theatre included the phrase "Beware of Imitations." I wonder what the need for this is?

Regarding the technical aspects of this film, it is necessary to say a few words. Although filming on the front lines is inherently difficult, there is little possibility of paying attention to technique. The editing of this film is comparatively "systematic," but it lacks the power of "contrast," and the enemy's brutality is also rarely exposed. In other words, it does not more clearly show the arduousness of the Volunteer Army's combat. The lighting is not clear enough, which is naturally because lighting cannot be used on the battlefield, but the film stock is also a major factor. Due to the small company's lack of capital, the equipment is not sophisticated, and the camera shots appear dull and inflexible. The subtitles are too blurred, and what the subtitles tell the audience is only a narrow national concept, without further grasping the greater national significance. In fact, the entire subject matter neglects the demands of the vast majority of people who are directly trampled under the iron heel of imperialism.

However, we should forgive it one hundred and twenty percent. In such difficult work, being able to achieve such results is already enough to satisfy us. Moreover, this is an anti-imperialist film. Therefore, I still, like after watching Nine Star Company's "Northeast Volunteer Army: A Bloody War History" (please refer to yesterday's film review in this publication), advise the people of Shanghai to use the money they would spend on other films to see this film, to understand the suffering of our weak nation with the interest of cinematic entertainment, and to resolutely strive for the future of our Chinese nation.

Statement of Opinions

News of the Current Situation That Should Be Disseminated on the Silver Screen 266

— Xue Fan

Foreign invaders are penetrating deep, and the national crisis is increasingly urgent. We, the people in the rear, still have enough to eat, enough to wear, and even enough entertainment. Therefore, some people say that the people in the rear are indulging in entertainment and have simply forgotten the endangered state... There are also some people who defend entertainment, saying... "Entertainment does not forget saving the country, saving the country does not forget entertainment," such as the New World's charity performance to aid the Northeast Volunteer Army this time, which embodies the meaning of saving the country in entertainment. I believe that both opinions have considerable reasons. Those who talk loftily about saving the country do not necessarily have to be hostile to entertainment, because on the one hand, engaging in serious work to save the country, and on the other hand, engaging in a very small amount of relaxing entertainment, cannot really be considered inappropriate. If soldiers on the front lines sing operas and chat in the trenches after charging and fighting at close quarters, we shouldn't call their actions insane, should we?

One day, I was watching a movie at a certain cinema. After about an hour of screening, there was a ten-minute break as usual, and then the screening continued... But before the screening, shockingly projected on the screen was a piece of alarming news, writing... "Jiukou has fallen, and many of our soldiers and civilians have been killed or injured. Our army is currently deploying defenses at a certain location, making a firm defense." Everyone in the theater sighed incessantly upon seeing this news. When everyone was fully focused on the plot of the film, suddenly came a piece of news about the national crisis, as if everyone had taken a refreshing medicine! I believe that if cinemas can take advantage of such opportunities to inject news of the current situation and news of the national crisis into the hearts of every viewer in such a clever way, this matter is worthy of praise and encouragement!

A Brief History of Mr. Tang Xiaodan, Set Designer at Tianyi Film Company 267

— Qing

Tang Xiaodan, a native of Fujian, is 24 years old, possesses fine features, and is a young and promising youth. In his early years, he studied in Japan, delving into aesthetics and architecture, both of which he mastered well. After returning to China, he held a position at Shanghai China Commercial Art Advertising Company, and his reputation grew. For a time, people flocked to him to design architectural patterns and advertising artwork. During the "January 28th" Incident last year, Shanghai became a war zone, and the company happened to be located in the war zone, sacrificing itself for the national crisis. Mr. Tang then joined Tianyi Film Company as the director of set design, creating novel and magnificent structures, delicate Tang palaces, opening up a new record in the history of Tianyi Film Company. The Shao brothers, owners of the company, value him more than ever, regretting that they did not meet him sooner.

Recently, Xue Juexian, a well-known Cantonese opera actor, established the Southern Film Company in Shanghai in cooperation with Tianyi Film Company to film "Platinum Dragon," and Mr. Tang is serving as the director of this film. We hope that this artist will become a famous director in the future.

Overseas Star News 269

— Cun

According to an American Broadway film magazine... In the whole year of 1931, there were thirty-seven stars who got married in Hollywood. In the first nine months of last year, thirty-four of them and their wives or husbands went to court for divorce, planning to make new connections. Marrying and divorcing, what does it all mean to them!

After completing "Blonde Venus," Marlene Dietrich disappeared. Even the most well-informed reporters could not find her踪跡. Some spread rumors that she had been abandoned by her husband, and some even said that she had gone to Germany. But now news has come that Marlene hid because she was filming "Song of Songs" without Von Sternberg as her director.

Charlie Chaplin has long had the intention of filming a Napoleon film, but as time goes by, his depiction of this film seems to be under even more careful consideration. In fact, he is now telling several close friends that he will no longer make comedies. Therefore, many people believe that he will start filming sound films.

Child Star Li Keng 270

— Jiang Qing

Among the general movie stars in our country, the most lacking talent is child actors. Zheng Xiaoqiu is now the mainstay of the Star Film Company's leading men, but the golden age of Er Chun [unclear]—the most prosperous time of martial arts films—has also passed. This Chinese Jackie Coogan-like figure has not yet emerged.

In the Lianhua Film Company's film "Humanity" last year, we discovered a brilliant talent—Li Keng, who was highly praised by the audience. He is only five years old this year, speaks fluent Cantonese, and is innocent, lively, and exceptionally cute. He is the beloved son of Li Minwei, the head of the Lianhua Film Company's first studio. Since "Humanity" was released, he will soon be filming "Childhood China," starring him. His Mandarin pronunciation is also very accurate. The Yong'an Company on Nanjing Road once invited him to sing on the radio.

Stone from Another Mountain

High-Heeled Leather Shoes and Military Maps in "Adventures in the War Zone" 271

— Xiao Yuhong

I deeply know that there are many areas where the Chinese film industry has its hardships, where the will is there but the strength is not enough, so film critics should also be understanding and not overly critical. However, small details within the realm of possibility should also be paid attention to. For example, in "Adventures in the War Zone," there seem to be two points that are not in line with reason:

Because Ding Mingxia ventured into the war zone, she changed into a villager's outfit. However, when she was imprisoned and voluntarily surrendered, after taking off her long old cloth socks, a pair of high-heeled leather shoes suddenly appeared. This seems inexplicable! It is impossible to wear high-heeled shoes with long old cloth socks and then wear men's shoes. If you say they were temporarily found in the bandit camp, that is also unreasonable.

Ding Mingxia's stolen military map is a major key to the entire drama, but we need to know what kind of map she stole? I can swear that what she stole was a very ordinary map of China, which is also unreasonable. It would be a great joke to plan a military action in a certain place on a very ordinary map of China. Moreover, Ding Mingxia stole it back with great difficulty, and the officials praised each other and regarded it as a great achievement!

The above two points are not nitpicking on practical matters. I wonder what the director thinks?

Dimples and Smiles 272

— Cheng

The beautiful dimples on either side of a woman's lips are called dimples. Also called smiles. Although the names are different, the intention is actually the same. Pears are sweet and juicy. Wine is fine wine, and in general, both are lovely and delicious. On the 16th of this publication, I saw Yuan Jun's contribution and felt that Hu Shan's words and speech had the flavor of competing with her older sister Hu Die for dimples. In fact, dear sister, don't compete, because there are two ways to say that beautiful dimple. Let's just call them... pear dimples Die, smile dimples Shan, okay. In this way, not only will each have a unique banner, which can make people pay special attention, but also there is a concept of standing side by side and achieving eternal fame! I wonder if other stars, such as the three Liang sisters, have any common characteristics? I must ask all the viewers to pay more attention!

The Story of the "Match King" (14) 273

— Translated by Xi Meng

Antoniu Skarazzi

319 rue de Rochechouart, Paris

One day a fishing boat towed into the harbor of a small island in the Baltic Sea. A man ran down from the boat, a small Italian man with a cunning look on his face. The fishing boat unloaded the guest and sailed away. After the man waited for the boat to leave, he picked up a small path and walked towards an empty summer house. When he arrived, he knocked on the door. The door was opened by Paul Kreuger. He opened the door, pulled the man inside, and the door closed tightly again.

"Do you want to buy some important documents from me?" the Italian asked.

"Let me see them first," Paul said. "There's no one else here." Paul saw the Italian pull out a rubber-coated bag from his side.

"Here are fifty Italian government treasury bonds," he slowly opened the bag, "each with a face value of one million." He placed them in Paul's hand.

"Sir, this is as good as the real thing, or even better," he said, his cunning gaze fixed on Paul's eyes. "Sir, how many do you want?"

"I want all fifty," Paul said decisively.

The Italian was suddenly surprised beyond his expectations when he heard this. He thought an opportunity to rip someone off had come. Moreover, with this large amount of fake bonds in his possession, he had a hold on him, and he could look for him at any time, a truly good customer to eat from for life.

Paul looked at the Italian and smiled strangely.

"Skarazzi, I'll pay you five thousand dollars now to show my sincerity in doing business with you. The rest of the money will be paid in Paris tomorrow. What do you think?"

"Very good, very good, sir," the Italian replied.

Paul took out his wallet, pulled out five one-thousand-dollar bills, and the Italian received them, inspected them repeatedly, nodded, and put them away.

"I'll take you ashore by the way," Paul said to him. "It shouldn't be difficult for you to enter Sweden, right?" He asked casually on purpose. Skarazzi laughed.

"I issue my own passport and sign my own name. No one knows I've entered Sweden."

In Paul's eyes, a strange light shone. He couldn't be more satisfied. What he wanted to know was that no one knew he was in Sweden.

The two of them stepped into the speedboat together. With money in hand, Skarazzi sat happily and openly at the stern of the boat, which sped through the waves like lightning. Suddenly, Paul Kreuger turned the wheel – Skarazzi cried out, rolled into the water, waves splashed everywhere, and the man was nowhere to be seen. Kreuger didn't even turn his head to look and continued to speed away. He went ashore very peacefully by himself.
